\DoxyCodeLine{449 DOCTEST\_INTERFACE \textcolor{keyword}{extern} \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} is\_running\_in\_test;}
\DoxyCodeLine{450 }
\DoxyCodeLine{451 \textcolor{comment}{// A 24 byte string class (can be as small as 17 for x64 and 13 for x86) that can hold strings with length}}
\DoxyCodeLine{452 \textcolor{comment}{// of up to 23 chars on the stack before going on the heap -\/ the last byte of the buffer is used for:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{453 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ "{}is small"{} bit -\/ the highest bit -\/ if "{}0"{} then it is small -\/ otherwise its "{}1"{} (128)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{454 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ if small -\/ capacity left before going on the heap -\/ using the lowest 5 bits}}
\DoxyCodeLine{455 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ if small -\/ 2 bits are left unused -\/ the second and third highest ones}}
\DoxyCodeLine{456 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ if small -\/ acts as a null terminator if strlen() is 23 (24 including the null terminator)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{457 \textcolor{comment}{//              and the "{}is small"{} bit remains "{}0"{} ("{}as well as the capacity left"{}) so its OK}}
\DoxyCodeLine{458 \textcolor{comment}{// Idea taken from this lecture about the string implementation of facebook/folly -\/ fbstring}}
\DoxyCodeLine{459 \textcolor{comment}{// https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=kPR8h4-\/qZdk}}
\DoxyCodeLine{460 \textcolor{comment}{// TODO:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{461 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ optimizations -\/ like not deleting memory unnecessarily in operator= and etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{462 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ resize/reserve/clear}}
\DoxyCodeLine{463 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ substr}}
\DoxyCodeLine{464 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ replace}}
\DoxyCodeLine{465 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ back/front}}
\DoxyCodeLine{466 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ iterator stuff}}
\DoxyCodeLine{467 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ find \& friends}}
\DoxyCodeLine{468 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ push\_back/pop\_back}}
\DoxyCodeLine{469 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ assign/insert/erase}}
\DoxyCodeLine{470 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ relational operators as free functions -\/ taking const char* as one of the params}}
\DoxyCodeLine{471 \textcolor{keyword}{class }DOCTEST\_INTERFACE \mbox{\hyperlink{classdoctest_1_1String}{String}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{472 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{473     \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} len  = 24;      }
\DoxyCodeLine{474     \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} last = len -\/ 1; }
\DoxyCodeLine{475 }
\DoxyCodeLine{476     \textcolor{keyword}{struct }view \textcolor{comment}{// len should be more than sizeof(view) -\/ because of the final byte for flags}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3040 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3041 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_NO\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3042     \textcolor{keyword}{template} <\textcolor{keyword}{typename} T>}
\DoxyCodeLine{3043     \textcolor{keyword}{using} AtomicOrMultiLaneAtomic = std::atomic<T>;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3044 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#else }\textcolor{comment}{// DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_NO\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3045     \textcolor{comment}{// Provides a multilane implementation of an atomic variable that supports add, sub, load,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3046     \textcolor{comment}{// store. Instead of using a single atomic variable, this splits up into multiple ones,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3047     \textcolor{comment}{// each sitting on a separate cache line. The goal is to provide a speedup when most}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3048     \textcolor{comment}{// operations are modifying. It achieves this with two properties:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3049     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3050     \textcolor{comment}{// * Multiple atomics are used, so chance of congestion from the same atomic is reduced.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3051     \textcolor{comment}{// * Each atomic sits on a separate cache line, so false sharing is reduced.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3052     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3053     \textcolor{comment}{// The disadvantage is that there is a small overhead due to the use of TLS, and load/store}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3054     \textcolor{comment}{// is slower because all atomics have to be accessed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3055     \textcolor{keyword}{template} <\textcolor{keyword}{typename} T>}
\DoxyCodeLine{3056     \textcolor{keyword}{class }MultiLaneAtomic}
\DoxyCodeLine{3057     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3058         \textcolor{keyword}{struct }CacheLineAlignedAtomic}
\DoxyCodeLine{3059         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3060             std::atomic<T> atomic\{\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3061             \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} padding[DOCTEST\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS\_CACHE\_LINE\_SIZE -\/ \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(std::atomic<T>)];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3062         \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3063         CacheLineAlignedAtomic m\_atomics[DOCTEST\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS\_THREAD\_LANES];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3064 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3065         \textcolor{keyword}{static\_assert}(\textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(CacheLineAlignedAtomic) == DOCTEST\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS\_CACHE\_LINE\_SIZE,}
\DoxyCodeLine{3066                       \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}guarantee one atomic takes exactly one cache line"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{3067 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3068     \textcolor{keyword}{public}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{3069         T operator++() DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} fetch\_add(1) + 1; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3070 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3071         T operator++(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int}) DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} fetch\_add(1); \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3072 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3073         T fetch\_add(T arg, std::memory\_order order = std::memory\_order\_seq\_cst) DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3074             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} myAtomic().fetch\_add(arg, order);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3075         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3076 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3077         T fetch\_sub(T arg, std::memory\_order order = std::memory\_order\_seq\_cst) DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3078             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} myAtomic().fetch\_sub(arg, order);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3079         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3080 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3081         \textcolor{keyword}{operator} T() const DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} load(); \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3082 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3083         T load(std::memory\_order order = std::memory\_order\_seq\_cst) \textcolor{keyword}{const} DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3084             \textcolor{keyword}{auto} result = T();}
\DoxyCodeLine{3085             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(\textcolor{keyword}{auto} \textcolor{keyword}{const}\& c : m\_atomics) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3086                 result += c.atomic.load(order);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3087             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3088             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} result;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3089         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3090 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3091         T operator=(T desired) DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3092             store(desired);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3093             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} desired;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3094         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3095 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3096         \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} store(T desired, std::memory\_order order = std::memory\_order\_seq\_cst) DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3097             \textcolor{comment}{// first value becomes desired"{}, all others become 0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3098             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(\textcolor{keyword}{auto}\& c : m\_atomics) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3099                 c.atomic.store(desired, order);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3100                 desired = \{\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3101             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3102         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3103 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3104     \textcolor{keyword}{private}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{3105         \textcolor{comment}{// Each thread has a different atomic that it operates on. If more than NumLanes threads}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3106         \textcolor{comment}{// use this, some will use the same atomic. So performance will degrate a bit, but still}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3107         \textcolor{comment}{// everything will work.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3108         \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3109         \textcolor{comment}{// The logic here is a bit tricky. The call should be as fast as possible, so that there}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3110         \textcolor{comment}{// is minimal to no overhead in determining the correct atomic for the current thread.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3111         \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3112         \textcolor{comment}{// 1. A global static counter laneCounter counts continuously up.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3113         \textcolor{comment}{// 2. Each successive thread will use modulo operation of that counter so it gets an atomic}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3114         \textcolor{comment}{//    assigned in a round-\/robin fashion.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3115         \textcolor{comment}{// 3. This tlsLaneIdx is stored in the thread local data, so it is directly available with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3116         \textcolor{comment}{//    little overhead.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3117         std::atomic<T>\& myAtomic() DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3118             \textcolor{keyword}{static} std::atomic<size\_t> laneCounter;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3119             DOCTEST\_THREAD\_LOCAL \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} tlsLaneIdx =}
\DoxyCodeLine{3120                     laneCounter++ \% DOCTEST\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS\_THREAD\_LANES;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3121 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3122             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} m\_atomics[tlsLaneIdx].atomic;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3123         \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3678     \textcolor{keyword}{using namespace }detail;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3679     \textcolor{comment}{// matching of a string against a wildcard mask (case sensitivity configurable) taken from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3680     \textcolor{comment}{// https://www.codeproject.com/Articles/1088/Wildcard-\/string-\/compare-\/globbing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3681     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} wildcmp(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* wild, \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} caseSensitive) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3682         \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* cp = str;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3683         \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* mp = wild;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3684 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3685         \textcolor{keywordflow}{while}((*str) \&\& (*wild != \textcolor{charliteral}{'*'})) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3686             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}((caseSensitive ? (*wild != *str) : (tolower(*wild) != tolower(*str))) \&\&}
\DoxyCodeLine{3687                (*wild != \textcolor{charliteral}{'?'})) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3688                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3689             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3690             wild++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3691             str++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3692         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3693 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3694         \textcolor{keywordflow}{while}(*str) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3695             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(*wild == \textcolor{charliteral}{'*'}) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3696                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(!*++wild) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3697                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3698                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3699                 mp = wild;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3700                 cp = str + 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3701             \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}((caseSensitive ? (*wild == *str) : (tolower(*wild) == tolower(*str))) ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{3702                       (*wild == \textcolor{charliteral}{'?'})) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3703                 wild++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3704                 str++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3705             \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3706                 wild = mp;   }
\DoxyCodeLine{3707                 str  = cp++; }
\DoxyCodeLine{3708             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3709         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3710 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3711         \textcolor{keywordflow}{while}(*wild == \textcolor{charliteral}{'*'}) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3712             wild++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3713         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3714         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} !*wild;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3715     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3716 }

\DoxyCodeLine{4085     \textcolor{comment}{// running under the debugger or has a debugger attached post facto).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4086     \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} isDebuggerActive() \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4087         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}        mib[4];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4088         kinfo\_proc info;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4089         \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t}     size;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4090         \textcolor{comment}{// Initialize the flags so that, if sysctl fails for some bizarre}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4091         \textcolor{comment}{// reason, we get a predictable result.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4092         info.kp\_proc.p\_flag = 0;}

\DoxyCodeLine{4094         \textcolor{comment}{// we're looking for information about a specific process ID.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4095         mib[0] = CTL\_KERN;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4096         mib[1] = KERN\_PROC;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4097         mib[2] = KERN\_PROC\_PID;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4098         mib[3] = getpid();}
\DoxyCodeLine{4099         \textcolor{comment}{// Call sysctl.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4100         size = \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(info);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4101         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(sysctl(mib, DOCTEST\_COUNTOF(mib), \&info, \&size, 0, 0) != 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4102             std::cerr << \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\(\backslash\)nCall to sysctl failed -\/ unable to determine if debugger is active **\(\backslash\)n"{}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4103             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \textcolor{keyword}{false};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4104         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4105         \textcolor{comment}{// We're being debugged if the P\_TRACED flag is set.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4205     \textcolor{keyword}{struct }FatalConditionHandler}

\DoxyCodeLine{4207         \textcolor{keyword}{static} LONG CALLBACK handleException(PEXCEPTION\_POINTERS ExceptionInfo) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4208             \textcolor{comment}{// Multiple threads may enter this filter/handler at once. We want the error message to be printed on the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4209             \textcolor{comment}{// console just once no matter how many threads have crashed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4210             \textcolor{keyword}{static} std::mutex mutex;}

\DoxyCodeLine{4215                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} reported = \textcolor{keyword}{false};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4216                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} i = 0; i < DOCTEST\_COUNTOF(signalDefs); ++i) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{4218                             reportFatal(signalDefs[i].name);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4219                             reported = \textcolor{keyword}{true};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4220                             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4221                         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4222                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4223                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(reported == \textcolor{keyword}{false})}
\DoxyCodeLine{4224                         reportFatal(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Unhandled SEH exception caught"{}});}

\DoxyCodeLine{4226                         DOCTEST\_BREAK\_INTO\_DEBUGGER();}
\DoxyCodeLine{4227                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4228                 execute = \textcolor{keyword}{false};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4229             \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4236         FatalConditionHandler() \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4237             isSet = \textcolor{keyword}{true};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4238             \textcolor{comment}{// 32k seems enough for doctest to handle stack overflow,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4239             \textcolor{comment}{// but the value was found experimentally, so there is no strong guarantee}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4240             guaranteeSize = 32 * 1024;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4241             \textcolor{comment}{// Register an unhandled exception filter}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4242             previousTop = SetUnhandledExceptionFilter(handleException);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4243             \textcolor{comment}{// Pass in guarantee size to be filled}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4244             SetThreadStackGuarantee(\&guaranteeSize);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4245 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4246             \textcolor{comment}{// On Windows uncaught exceptions from another thread, exceptions from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4247             \textcolor{comment}{// destructors, or calls to std::terminate are not a SEH exception}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4248 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4249             \textcolor{comment}{// The terminal handler gets called when:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4250             \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ std::terminate is called FROM THE TEST RUNNER THREAD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4251             \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ an exception is thrown from a destructor FROM THE TEST RUNNER THREAD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4252             original\_terminate\_handler = std::get\_terminate();}
\DoxyCodeLine{4253             std::set\_terminate([]() DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4254                 reportFatal(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Terminate handler called"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{4255                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(isDebuggerActive() \&\& !g\_cs-\/>no\_breaks)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4256                     DOCTEST\_BREAK\_INTO\_DEBUGGER();}
\DoxyCodeLine{4257                 std::exit(EXIT\_FAILURE); \textcolor{comment}{// explicitly exit -\/ otherwise the SIGABRT handler may be called as well}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4258             \});}
\DoxyCodeLine{4259 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4260             \textcolor{comment}{// SIGABRT is raised when:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4261             \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ std::terminate is called FROM A DIFFERENT THREAD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4262             \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ an exception is thrown from a destructor FROM A DIFFERENT THREAD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4263             \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ an uncaught exception is thrown FROM A DIFFERENT THREAD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4264             prev\_sigabrt\_handler = std::signal(SIGABRT, [](\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} signal) DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4265                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(signal == SIGABRT) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4266                     reportFatal(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}SIGABRT -\/ Abort (abnormal termination) signal"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{4267                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(isDebuggerActive() \&\& !g\_cs-\/>no\_breaks)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4268                         DOCTEST\_BREAK\_INTO\_DEBUGGER();}
\DoxyCodeLine{4269                     std::exit(EXIT\_FAILURE);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4270                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4271             \});}
\DoxyCodeLine{4272 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4273             \textcolor{comment}{// The following settings are taken from google test, and more}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4274             \textcolor{comment}{// specifically from UnitTest::Run() inside of gtest.cc}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4275 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4276             \textcolor{comment}{// the user does not want to see pop-\/up dialogs about crashes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4277             prev\_error\_mode\_1 = SetErrorMode(SEM\_FAILCRITICALERRORS | SEM\_NOALIGNMENTFAULTEXCEPT |}
\DoxyCodeLine{4278                                              SEM\_NOGPFAULTERRORBOX | SEM\_NOOPENFILEERRORBOX);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4279             \textcolor{comment}{// This forces the abort message to go to stderr in all circumstances.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4280             prev\_error\_mode\_2 = \_set\_error\_mode(\_OUT\_TO\_STDERR);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4281             \textcolor{comment}{// In the debug version, Visual Studio pops up a separate dialog}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4282             \textcolor{comment}{// offering a choice to debug the aborted program -\/ we want to disable that.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4283             prev\_abort\_behavior = \_set\_abort\_behavior(0x0, \_WRITE\_ABORT\_MSG | \_CALL\_REPORTFAULT);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4284             \textcolor{comment}{// In debug mode, the Windows CRT can crash with an assertion over invalid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4285             \textcolor{comment}{// input (e.g. passing an invalid file descriptor). The default handling}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4286             \textcolor{comment}{// for these assertions is to pop up a dialog and wait for user input.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4287             \textcolor{comment}{// Instead ask the CRT to dump such assertions to stderr non-\/interactively.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4288             prev\_report\_mode = \_CrtSetReportMode(\_CRT\_ASSERT, \_CRTDBG\_MODE\_FILE | \_CRTDBG\_MODE\_DEBUG);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4289             prev\_report\_file = \_CrtSetReportFile(\_CRT\_ASSERT, \_CRTDBG\_FILE\_STDERR);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4290         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4291 }

\DoxyCodeLine{4698     \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} trailingBytes(\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} c) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4699         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((c \& 0xE0) == 0xC0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4700             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4701         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4702         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((c \& 0xF0) == 0xE0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4703             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4704         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4705         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((c \& 0xF8) == 0xF0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4706             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4707         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4708         DOCTEST\_INTERNAL\_ERROR(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Invalid multibyte utf-\/8 start byte encountered"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{4709     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4710 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4711     uint32\_t headerValue(\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} c) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4712         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((c \& 0xE0) == 0xC0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4713             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} c \& 0x1F;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4714         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4715         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((c \& 0xF0) == 0xE0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4716             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} c \& 0x0F;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4717         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4718         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((c \& 0xF8) == 0xF0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4719             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} c \& 0x07;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4720         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4721         DOCTEST\_INTERNAL\_ERROR(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Invalid multibyte utf-\/8 start byte encountered"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{4722     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4723 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4724     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} hexEscapeChar(std::ostream\& os, \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} c) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4725         std::ios\_base::fmtflags f(os.flags());}
\DoxyCodeLine{4726         os << \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\(\backslash\)\(\backslash\)x"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4727             << std::uppercase << std::hex << std::setfill(\textcolor{charliteral}{'0'}) << std::setw(2)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4728             << \textcolor{keyword}{static\_cast<}\textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\textcolor{keyword}{>}(c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4729         os.flags(f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4730     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4731 }

\DoxyCodeLine{4733 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4734     XmlEncode::XmlEncode( std::string \textcolor{keyword}{const}\& str, ForWhat forWhat )}
\DoxyCodeLine{4735     :   m\_str( str ),}
\DoxyCodeLine{4736         m\_forWhat( forWhat )}
\DoxyCodeLine{4737     \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4738 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4739     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} XmlEncode::encodeTo( std::ostream\& os )\textcolor{keyword}{ const }\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4740         \textcolor{comment}{// Apostrophe escaping not necessary if we always use "{} to write attributes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4741         \textcolor{comment}{// (see: https://www.w3.org/TR/xml/\#syntax)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4742 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4743         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}( std::size\_t idx = 0; idx < m\_str.size(); ++ idx ) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4744             uchar c = m\_str[idx];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4745             \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (c) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4746             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'<'}:   os << \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\&lt;"{}}; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4747             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'\&'}:   os << \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\&amp;"{}}; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4748 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4749             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'>'}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{4750                 \textcolor{comment}{// See: https://www.w3.org/TR/xml/\#syntax}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4751                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (idx > 2 \&\& m\_str[idx -\/ 1] == \textcolor{charliteral}{']'} \&\& m\_str[idx -\/ 2] == \textcolor{charliteral}{']'})}
\DoxyCodeLine{4752                     os << \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\&gt;"{}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4753                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4754                     os << c;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4755                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4756 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4757             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)"{}'}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{4758                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (m\_forWhat == ForAttributes)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4759                     os << \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\&quot;"{}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4760                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4761                     os << c;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4762                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4763 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4764             \textcolor{keywordflow}{default}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{4765                 \textcolor{comment}{// Check for control characters and invalid utf-\/8}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4766 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4767                 \textcolor{comment}{// Escape control characters in standard ascii}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4768                 \textcolor{comment}{// see https://stackoverflow.com/questions/404107/why-\/are-\/control-\/characters-\/illegal-\/in-\/xml-\/1-\/0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4769                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (c < 0x09 || (c > 0x0D \&\& c < 0x20) || c == 0x7F) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4770                     hexEscapeChar(os, c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4771                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4772                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4773 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4774                 \textcolor{comment}{// Plain ASCII: Write it to stream}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4775                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (c < 0x7F) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4776                     os << c;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4777                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4778                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4779 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4780                 \textcolor{comment}{// UTF-\/8 territory}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4781                 \textcolor{comment}{// Check if the encoding is valid and if it is not, hex escape bytes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4782                 \textcolor{comment}{// Important: We do not check the exact decoded values for validity, only the encoding format}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4783                 \textcolor{comment}{// First check that this bytes is a valid lead byte:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4784                 \textcolor{comment}{// This means that it is not encoded as 1111 1XXX}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4785                 \textcolor{comment}{// Or as 10XX XXXX}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4786                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (c <  0xC0 ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{4787                     c >= 0xF8) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4788                     hexEscapeChar(os, c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4789                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4790                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4791 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4792                 \textcolor{keyword}{auto} encBytes = trailingBytes(c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4793                 \textcolor{comment}{// Are there enough bytes left to avoid accessing out-\/of-\/bounds memory?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4794                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (idx + encBytes -\/ 1 >= m\_str.size()) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4795                     hexEscapeChar(os, c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4796                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4797                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4798                 \textcolor{comment}{// The header is valid, check data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4799                 \textcolor{comment}{// The next encBytes bytes must together be a valid utf-\/8}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4800                 \textcolor{comment}{// This means: bitpattern 10XX XXXX and the extracted value is sane (ish)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4801                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} valid = \textcolor{keyword}{true};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4802                 uint32\_t value = headerValue(c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4803                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (std::size\_t n = 1; n < encBytes; ++n) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4804                     uchar nc = m\_str[idx + n];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4805                     valid \&= ((nc \& 0xC0) == 0x80);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4806                     value = (value << 6) | (nc \& 0x3F);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4807                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4808 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4809                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (}
\DoxyCodeLine{4810                     \textcolor{comment}{// Wrong bit pattern of following bytes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4811                     (!valid) ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{4812                     \textcolor{comment}{// Overlong encodings}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4813                     (value < 0x80) ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{4814                     (                 value < 0x800   \&\& encBytes > 2) || \textcolor{comment}{// removed "{}0x80 <= value \&\&"{} because redundant}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4815                     (0x800 < value \&\& value < 0x10000 \&\& encBytes > 3) ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{4816                     \textcolor{comment}{// Encoded value out of range}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4817                     (value >= 0x110000)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4818                     ) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4819                     hexEscapeChar(os, c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4820                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4821                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4822 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4823                 \textcolor{comment}{// If we got here, this is in fact a valid(ish) utf-\/8 sequence}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4824                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (std::size\_t n = 0; n < encBytes; ++n) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4825                     os << m\_str[idx + n];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4826                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4827                 idx += encBytes -\/ 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4828                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4829             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4830         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4831     \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{6369 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6370             \textcolor{comment}{// random\_shuffle implementation}}

\DoxyCodeLine{6372             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} i = testArray.size() -\/ 1; i > 0; -\/-\/i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6373                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} idxToSwap = std::rand() \% (i + 1); \textcolor{comment}{// NOLINT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6374 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6375                 \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keyword}{auto} temp = first[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{6376 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6377                 first[i]         = first[idxToSwap];}
\DoxyCodeLine{6378                 first[idxToSwap] = temp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6379             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6380         \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(p-\/>order\_by.compare(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}none"{}}, \textcolor{keyword}{true}) == 0) \{}
